< text>
Friendly staff, good music from the digital Jukebox. I ordered the club sandwich and was delighted to see thick cuts of meat that look like they came off of a slicer on the thick setting. Veggies were nice and crisp, and the bacon was very crunchy and nice. The bread is  buttered and toasted. This is a nice sized sandwich and I am pleased.  I recommend that you come give the place a try. Good beer selection as well.<//text>

He was very happy, his experience was positive, and he was confident that I would have the same experience.

I called Aava Dental in Foothill Ranch and spoke with Angela.  Angela allayed my fears and eased my mind as to what to expect. In addition, there were so many positive views on Google.  I had some intermittent molar pain and I needed a cleaning as well.  I went to the Santa Ana location. As soon as I walked in I was warmly greeted by Angela. I met Rebecca who took my xrays and walked me through the process.  Then, there is Dr. Weber, who is THE BEST DENTIST I have ever had in my life.  I thank God for her.  I am in my early 50's so that is saying a lot. It turned out I had five cavities and my cleaning was easy. Dr. Weber and her staff know I am a "chicken" when it comes to being in that dental chair and being worked on.
Here is a comprehensive list of what I went through.  It's also the little things that mean so much.
-Verbal welcome greeting from every person. Office was decorated with fall season theme
-Your name is on a welcome board (Welcome Sandra!). My husband had that also
-Top of the line X-ray machine where you stand and the machine "talks" to you while taking images of your teeth
-Gentle inserts of x-rays of your mouth
-While in the dentist chair you can request your kind of music to make you relaxed
-Goggles for your eyes so I can feel protected
-Dr. Weber tells you exactly what she will do.  She is gentle and comforting when she had to numb me. My oral cavity does not get numb quickly so I was numbed the maximum number of times. She is so gentle, had so much patience, and professional!
-There were pictures of my lovely cavity-filled teeth.  I recognized my teeth immediately! She described what happens if cavities don't get treated.  She was really fast when treating the cavities.
-She explained what teeth are and how to care for them
-They talk while working on your teeth so there is distraction that your mouth open and teeth are worked on
-She explained that I may have a traumatized nerve on my molar. There was no major cavity on that tooth and we narrowed it down to what it may be.
-Rebecca was very gentle with that suction tube.  (Other dentists I had been to would stick that tube and poke the inside of my mouth harshly)
-There is a detailed list of charges that you get at the end of your visit.  None of that "surprise" billing that you get from other dental practices.

I personally like that this is an all female staff.  To me, it's way different than having a male dentist and female staff.
I highly recommend Aava Dental Santa Ana and Foothill Ranch with Dr. Weber, Rebecca and Angela!< /Text><gmap_id>0x80dcd97c2030064b:0xff580d538eba4473</gmap_id>< rating>

<pictures>None< /pictures><rating>4< /rating><Text>Stopped in to grab a bite to eat after running errands.  Ordered the Vacon Sensation Omelette with Pancakesü•û.

Due to Post Pandemic climate, condiments aren't readily available so, don't forget to ask for desired items.  Understandable but still a little annoying because if you forget to ask for something, you'll may have a wait getting the attention of the server.

This IHOP is in a good location but the Management should rethink the interior design/layout because it's pretty tight that present a problem with the flow of traffic all around with servers putting the final touches on dishes,  Associates trying to maneuver to bust tables, customers trying to pay, customers entering and exiting...too tight and congested especially with the Cashier Station right in the same area.

Food was nice and hot, I typically request hot syrup for my Pancakesü•û because there have been times when the cooks finish the Pancakes and they end up sitting on the counter.

Now, IHOP was a staple for our familyüë™ so I miss the true original fluffy Buttermilk Pancakes.  Not sure if the recipe changed over the years (I'm sure it has) but their definitely not fluffy through and through, a little hard along the edges.  They usually come apart when lifting to butter the individual pancake so, I focus on the center portions and call it a wrap.

A decent experience but the downside for me is the configuration of the space to create a more fluid and unpedded traffic flow.

Enjoy!<//Text><Response>None</Response>< user>
